The clerk asked if I wanted to vacate the unit or let them fix the problem. Right, like they are going to get around to fixing it before it rains again. Besides, it's moldy in there! Told him I wanted a new unit.

He says he will take pictures of the damage and he will meet us at the unit as soon as he's done renting a unit to the guy ahead of us. We go to the unit and wait. And wait. And wait.

Finally even my wife's patience wears out and she walks back to the office and he tells her he thought we left??? Shelly tells him we've been waiting for 45 minutes! So he says he'll be there "right after helping his current customer." A different customer than was there before.

15 minutes later and we're STILL waiting at the unit. At this point I wouldn't have taken a FREE room from them. We packed up all the damaged stuff (lost an artificial tree and some Easter stuff to water damage and mold) and left. When we were leaving the guy was helping yet ANOTHER customer. No, pay no attention to the people who have been waiting for an hour!

<Rate>None<//Rate>< review>
The rooms were clean and the hotel was just the right size... not a gigantic mega franchise but small enough to make the breakfast not seem overly crowded. The staff were very professional and old photos of Davis in the lobby were a classy touch. Kudos for the all you can eat fresh fruit, and all you can drink fresh ice water and coffee. Breakfast covered all the basics, even oatmeal which was delicious. Only setback was that the elevator was out of service twice but it was repaired by the time we checked out, and was not a big hassle when it was out of commission since the property is only two stories tall plus the ground floor. Keep in mind that if you require a copy of your receipt/folio at checkout then you should book directly with La Quinta. Overall a very pleasant experience during our week-long stay.</review>

<review>This place was great! I had to stay there during a business trip, so when I got back to the hotel, I was exhausted. The bed was comfortable, the air was chilly (great!), and we had Direct TV!

The blinds are a bit weird, as in you can't draw the thick blinds across the whole window. Expect a lot of light. Also, don't get naked in front of the window. When i stepped out for a smoke, I realized that folks could probably see me through my window LOL!

If you need white noise to fall asleep, bring a fan. The AC's fan doesn't run outside of the AC's cycle. so there was a lot of silence.

The continental breakfast was great. They had boiled eggs, which impressed me. Usually these free breakfasts don't have any source of protein, but this one did. Had a good selection of cereal, muffins, fruits, and other things.

The best for me was that I left my laptop there after checking out. DOH! When I came back to get it, they had actually plugged it in and charged it for me! I'm was so impressed by this! I used the full charge during the day too, so I was very thankful.

Great stay, great folks, great deal. Would stay again.</review><Gmap_id>0x808529701b618117:0x8fe4cab42e48b51a< /Gmap_id>< user_name>

< review>
My dog has been treated well there, Dr Appel, Dr Tom, and vet tech Erin have been really great. But there are 2 main things that would make me think twice about going back again.

1. Occasionally I'll call in and speak with a specific person who is ALWAYS argumentative and rude and treats like everything I have to say is a fight. This person is always difficult to speak with because they speak over me where I can't even finish my sentences. (You probably know who it is.)

2. The price of medication can be grossly overpriced. I understand they're a small business and I wouldn't expect them to price match if they are to make a profit, but I checked prices of a few locations and they're grossly up-charging more than 1000% on one of my dogs pills. ONE THOUSAND PERCENT, you read that right.
Example:
500mg Cephalexin 84 capsules @ Singing Hills Vet charged $170.62
500mg Cephalexin 84 capsules on Chewy.com costs $16.80

So while I do like the clinic and I feel that my dog is very cared for, I do feel like they're taking advantage of worried pet parents. When I called in to ask for literally anything to make up for the cost, it was such a big argument to even get my point across. Hell, they could have thrown in a free dog treat and just said "sorry!" but instead it was just excuses and quite frankly they were extremely rude.< /review>

< text>
Very compassionate.  We recently had to euthanize an 18 year old cat and they did it with dignity.  They have a room (with lots of tissue) to wait in. <rating>4<//rating>< Review>
Good location. If I was still a childless adult, this would be a 5 star rating. As that is no longer the case, it is now 4 star, here's why. We have a six month old baby. The tables can fit 6 people, however, the depth between seat back and table are very narrow even without holding a somewhat squirmy child. Also the metal pole under the table bruised the knees of both my husband and father in law entering the seating area, both are about 5'11". There are 2 alternate seating areas as options (two round tables in the back, or what looks like a wheelchair accessible bar at the front, both with moveable chairs.
We've come to this location 3 times now, good experience each time. Open promptly. Friendly, knowledgeable staff that could help us decipher between the best Italian options. Great customer service which goes a long way with us. Good salt n vinegar chips. Restroom is clean and stocked. Downside is there is no  baby changing station. There is a wheelchair ramp for the sidewalk in front of the store, with rail. Two wheelchair accessible spots directly in front, and multiple others.< /Review>

< Text>
First, the music is way too loud and a complete distraction for an eating experience.  Hearing AC/DC wailing away at "Back in Black" is not conducive to a decent dining experience.  Turn the music OFF.

Second, I don't want to see the "potty humor" all over your bathroom depicting various scenes of urination and defecation.  Completely unnecessary, stupid and, again, not conducive to any sort of dining experience.

Third, I don't want to hear your staff whining (to me and other staff) that an employee left and that they're swamped. Yes, the restaurant was busy, but only because it was the dinner hour.

Fourth, I know you are too busy to answer the phone, but does your phone have to be so loud that it's heard over the entire restaurant?  AC/DC interrupted by a loud, constantly ringing phone that apparently doesn't have message or mute capability.  Sheesh.  I changed my "for here" order to "to go" because I couldn't stand the blaring noise in the restaurant.  You're going to make your employees and customers deaf!

The sandwich was okay, but skimpy.

I actually went here for the 1st time because I SUPPORT legal hunting, but I won't be coming back again.  I'll be hunting for a different sandwich shop.<//Text>

< review>
What a great place to eat! I've yet to be disappointed when eating here. The atmosphere is great for a casual dining establishment,  the service is always better than average and the food is done well. The carnitas are crispy, the rice is flavorful (like a Puerto Rican style, much better than the bland rice most places have) the rellenos are well done, great soup and salad dressing, etc. Its not the greasy burrito place I love, but it's great for sit down mexican dinner.

I reccomend any night of the week.</review>

<Name>ROB McAuliffe</Name><Date>1532449746124</Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Took the short drive to downtown Davis from Sacramento today and had lunch with my wife. We elected to sit outside on the patio and enjoy the nice breeze under the shade of trees and umbrellas. Warm chips and salsa arrived quickly as did our ice tea. Plenty of selections available as we scanned the menu and sighted the Amtrack station across the street. My wife had the tostada bowl chicken salad and I chose the  huevous with steak and refried beans. Food was seasoned perfectly and was quite flavorful. Good sized portions and our ice teas were refilled promptly.  A large fountain outside the entrance kept passersby parents and children interested, as they stopped to walk across the intersection. We received excellent food and service, despite there being a large baby shower party on the patio as well. We definitely plan to return and I strongly recommend you visit Tres Hermanas in Davis and experience this for yourself.<//Review>
